<Author>MsProzac
<Content>Crazy Woman at Hotel Staff Saves Day I'm a frequent traveler to Hawaii as I am a medical patient who participates in cancer studies. I'm an Ohana and more often than not have had an exceptional experience at the Ocean Resort.I have read most of the reviews of the Ocean Resort and while it's true it's an older hotel, needs a little work and isn't a five star hotel I've never seen bugs or had a problem until this last trip.I was staying in the Pali Tower with a room that had a view of Diamond Head and partial ocean. My last night there I was eating dinner on my patio, watching the sunset around Diamond Head and taking some photos. I captured some great shots of jets as they came around Diamond Head and was enjoying a great meal. Across the way from me was the Ocean Resorts Diamond Tower. There was a woman on her patio who kept staring at me while I was eating. It made me uncomfortable. Pretty soon I noticed that the entire clan was staring at me. I tried to ignore them.All of the sudden there was a bang on my door and I asked who it was. It was the police. I opened the door and there was an Ocean Resort Rep and several officers. At first they thought they had the wrong room, but when they asked if I was taking photos and I said yes they requested to enter my room. I allowed them to and was informed that the person in the Diamond Tower had reported that I was stalking them and taking photos of them. At that time I offered to show management and the police my photos but they didn't feel it was necessary. They left and I thought things were settled. However the person in Diamond tower continued to watch my every move and I finally tried to talk to them. It was hard to hear them because of the noise, but they were not satisfied that I had not been arrested. I requested that management come back to my room, which they did, and the cops came back as well. I then showed them my photos and the cops said to not worry about it. Later on that night the Ocean Resort rep who had witnessed the whole thing came up and apologized to me for the whole mess. She was very kind and thought the situation was really outrageous. She wanted to try to make the rest of my stay wonderful, but I was leaving the next morning. I did ask her to make sure someone addressed that woman in the other building because I felt totally harassed and I was simply taking pictures and trying to enjoy my last night there.For all the negatives that have been written about the Ocean Resort I want to go on record as saying that they were exceptional in my situation and I will stay there again in November when I return. I just hope that by that time that lady is in therapy and no where near me.And for the record, my room was clean, the view spectacular and I really didn't notice anything too bad except for the smell of carpet cleaner in one of the elevators.

<Author>OldGuy57
<Content>Tired..Tired..Tired... We stayed at this hotel in August '05, not much positive to say about this property. You would expect the staff at check-in to be helpful, but not in this case. The front desk staff we're more annoyed that it was busy than they were helpful, basically said 'your room isn't ready-come back at 3:00 (it was 12:30)' and pointed to the valet area of the lobby. The lobby was full of luggage all tied together, it was the valet's job to give you a claim ticket, then tie your luggage into the group. When we returned and finally got a room (they couldn't find our reservation, even though we had just checked in three hours prior) it was not quite what we had been led to believe from the web-site. The building is very 'tired' and in need of alot maintenance, from the filthy carpets to the paint chipping and peeling off the walls. In our room I had to put the sliding glass door back on its track just to get it to open and close, both lamps were broken and held straight by propping the shades against the wall, the railing on the lanai was missing screws and brackets loose. We had 'upgraded' when we booked the trip to an 'superior kitchenette' from a standard, I'd hate to see what was in the standard because the superior included a two burner cooktop, a 'small' coffee pot without any coffee or filters ever supplied during an eight day stay and a small dorm-style refrigerator. The only positive was that housekeeping would work around your schedule, except the second day when we had to ask for clean towels, they had taken the used ones but didn't replace them with clean..?..stated they had 'run out' of towels, but did supply some by the time we returned. Avoid the valet parking if possible, $10 a day and you could wait for 1/2 hour to get your car, talked with one guest who's vehicle was damaged by the valet, no apology-just handed him a form to fill out. If you just want a place to shower between trips to the beach and shopping this might be for you, if your looking to relax this one isn't for you, from the 'postage stamp' size pools (4-6 people max) to the SLOWEST elevators in Hawaii, its just not a very good property.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Very Good Hotel at Reasonable Price My wife and I stayed at the Ocean Resort while on a mini-vacation. The room was comfortable. Had a balcony with partial view of the ocean. The hotel is a block in, so if you don't get a room on an upper floor facing south, you have no ocean view. Even so, the views are partially blocked by hotels between the Ocean Resort and the ocean. The staff was very cordial and helpful. We only ate breakfasts in the restaurant and they were very good and reasonably priced. The only negative, if there is one, is the parking situation. You have to reserve a spot in the small underground garage on a day to day basis. But there is a parking garage across and up the street, less than a block away, and its cheaper to park there. So parking wasn't really an issue. All in all, it was a great stay.

<Author>rosensuesue
<Content>No problems and the price is right My husband and I just returned from 11 nights at the Ocean Resort Hotel. As budget-consicous travelers, we found this hotel to very adequately meet our expectations. Our only regret is that we were unable to upgrade to a room with kitchenette and one at a higher level with a view. They said they were too full to move us, and we were there for 11 nights. Our room was on the second floor with no view, but had a bright room with a king size bed, small table with 2 chairs and a balcony with two chairs. We moved the table to the balcony for breakfast each day and enjoyed the beatiful Oahu mornings. There was a small refrigerator that worked just fine for milk, juice and fresh pineapple. The cleaning service was excellent, the maids friendly, and we never had to make any complaints. The TV worked fine, and we never noticed bothersome noise during the night. We're not fans of airconditioning, but used it serveral times and it worked fine. Being on the second floor, there was no wait for elevators and we had the option of taking the stairway. Never saw a bug. The lobby is bright and clean, though front desk staff could be a bit more friendly. Only had one breakfast in the hotel restaurant and found it to be adequate though nothing special. Overall, I would not hesitate to stay there again. Location is it's chief asset followed by it's affordable rates. It's less than a 5-minute walk to the beach and 2 minutes to the bus stop. As others have said, if you want fancy, go to a more expensive place. If you want a comfortable, clean, economical place to sleep in between days of exploring and enjoying Oahu, give the Ocean Resort Hotel a try. We liked it; hope you do too.  
<Date>Mar 3, 2005

<Author>VictorianTea
<Content>Nice Hotel except for the power thing... We stayed at the Ocean Resort Hotel Waikiki from Feb. 8-22/05 and it was the best value (oceanview/top floor for the money) that we have ever had in Waikiki (it was our 5th trip, but first time at this hotel). We were there when the power failure happened (power off for 34 hours, no A/C for 64 hours) but were given the coupons for the restaurant and the promise of a 2-night credit as our trip was pre-paid (we actually have not seen this credit yet as we booked through Expedia). Overall, the rooms were cleaned everyday, new sheets/blankets/towels, etc., vacuumed everyday (except for the power failure days of course) and we found the check in staff to be helpful and very courteous. I was sort of expecting the worst from reading previous reviews of this hotel, however, I did not find any of the complaints people were talking about. Even the elevators (when the power was on) were working reasonably fast. We would definitely stay in this hotel again in the future.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Not a Bad Hotel Considering... I'd really like to give this hotel a 5, but I feel I would be doing an injustice to those who read these reviews if I did. The room was clean and freshly vacuumed when we arrived for our 8-day stay; however, I don't think they vacuumed again. They did, however, change sheets AND blankets while we were there.Unfortunately, the electicity went out in the hotel for a total of 36 hours--a transformer blew and from what I heard it was due to the fact that the other one was extremely old. I don't hold the Hotel responsible for this as it could happen anywhere, except maybe at a brand new hotel. During the 36 hours of no electicity, the staff was helpful and offered glow sticks, free dinner coupons and showers at a nearby hotel, and had the electric company string lights in the lobby so it wasn't completely dark. We were only affected slightly--no hot water, no ability to cook food, and no TV (but we were in Hawaii, so who watches TV anyway). The only thing that upset me was that we had just purchased $50 worth of food and most of it needed to be thrown out. When I mentioned this to the front desk upon checkout, she asked if we still had the receipt (I'm guessing to give us a refund), however, I had already thrown it out. The free dinner coupons at a nearby hotel made up for the lost food, but it wasn't quite an even swap as the other hotel's buffet was meager. They also gave us a 2-hour late checkout after I complained a bit. We chose this hotel because it had a kitchenette and we could save money on food. The first night we were there, the hotplate didn't get hot enough to boil water (it was very old), so I mentioned it to the front desk. In a matter of a few hours, a maintenance man was in our room and replaced the hotplate with a brand new one. We had no problems after that. The kitchenette was well stocked with your basic essentials.For what we paid to stay here, it was worth the money. It wasn't the Marriott next door, but it lived up to my expectations. Most hotels in this area are $250 or more a night. This was around $89. The room was spacious, had a nice dining table with four chairs, pleasant view, and the shower was clean with no signs of mildew. I never saw one bug, fly, or any other creepy crawlers. If it hadn't been for the electrical problem, this hotel would have ranked well above average for the price.  
<Date>Feb 22, 2005

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>A clean place to crash I read many reviews on the Ocean Resort after we booked the hotel so I was kind of prepared and didn't set my expectations high. As many mentioned it's very outdated and in need of some repair, but who goes to Hawaii for the appearance of a lobby right? Once you get into your room you'll find that it's clean. Housekeeping did a great job and we were very satisfied with how clean it was. The air conditioner worked great for the most part. It did turn off during the day twice, the service man would just flip a breaker and it would be up and running the next second. The balcony was nice, great for reading in the morning. Most importantly...it was a clean place to stay, all you do is crash there anyways after a long day of playing. So save your money and enjoy spending it elsewhere. We didn't like the restaurant at the hotel too much, theres so many to choose from in Waikiki...not a problem. Try Ezo Giku Ramen right down the way for some great California Rolls and Wonton Ramen Soup..Cheeseburger in Paradise for a fun atomosphere...and Roy's Restaurant for a Romantic Ocean View Dinner (make reservations there).Unlike the last review, I do suggest renting a car...it's the only way to see the Island at your own pace. There's so much more to see and do outside of Waikiki and just cruising down the coast and stopping wherever you want is soo great!! Try renting at Thrify car rental- $40 a day for an economy car. Park diagnol to the Ocean Resort at the Banyan Hotel for $7 bucks a day.You can also catch bus 22 (stops across the street in front of the Marriot) to Hanauma Bay and Diamond Head Crater for $2 a person one way. I just got back Saturday and am already dreaming of going back....

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Easy place for a two week stay on a limited budget Our group of 10 stayed at the hotel from Nov. 18 till Dec.1 while members of the team trained and particiapated in the 2004 Honolulu International Karate Championship. We were one of several sports teams that stayed at the hotel during the time period as well as several tour groups from other countries as well as the mainland.....This hotel is an older place that is located across from the Marriot....if you want to pay Marriott prices...walk across the street and you get the same view....It is not a Motel 6 nor is it a Marriott...it is an older budget hotel that is located across the street from the main bus routes, next to the ABC store, Wolfgang Puck Express and a great Tiki bar/resturant at the Aston Hotel as well as around the corner from Starbucks, Cold Stone Creamery and another ABC. The beach is one block away and an easy walk...Even if you do not need the refrig/kitchette- go ahead and get a room in the Pali tower with them...rooms are much bigger....Realize that the majority of rooms have double ( full size) beds in the rooms and not queens or king size like at most hotel....also in the other tower ( I can't remember the name) the beds are twins and the rooms are much smaller. We loved to sit out on the balcony and read the newspaper and drink coffee in the mornings or to watch the lights at night....The price was great and met the needs of our team for 13 nights...if we stayed at the Marriott, our rooms would probably have been much nicer but our trip would have probably lasted only 3 nights and left at least five members at home because of the expense. Most folks are only in their rooms to sleep and shower....why pay more....Oh and by the way- I am a Marriott member and normally when traveling with family/business- that is my choice of where to stay...but this trip was different and the needs of the group( mainly teenagers and young adults with very limited budgets) were met quite adquately by the Ocean Resorts and its friendly staff...  
<Date>Dec 13, 2004

<Content>You get what you pay for We stayed here for 7 nights - late Oct 04. We got the Diamond Tower Floor 15. Room was clean but dated. <Author>Inakika44
<Content>Had an awesome stay I just returned from a 9 day stay at the Ocean Resort. I was there from Nov. 4th -13th. Check in was quick and efficient, we were in our room within 15 minutes after arriving. Our room (1539) was clean and spacious. We stayed in the Pali tower and had a small kitchenette. Yes, the stove is a double burner hot plate, the microwave was small as was the refrigerator, but it was more then adequate for my husband and myself. We cooked our own breakfast almost every morning and we also cooked dinner a few times as well. We could eat on our lanai which had a beautiful view of Diamond Head. It was a 5 minute walk to the beach and the location is close to several restaurants and the main drag Kalakaua. It was great to be able to access all the shops so easily and the close proximity to Diamond Head is a plus as well. You have to check out Teddy's Burger place which is off of Kalakaua and Kapahulu (walk up Kapahulu for a minute, it's on the left) The burgers are delicious and HUGE! I have been to Waikiki 5 times, staying at several different hotels, the Ocean Resort is where I will stay next year on visit number 6. The manager even sent my husband and myself a beautiful gift basket when she found out we were celebrating our 21st anniversary. To top it off, my husband lost his med. alert bracelet in the room and I got a call letting me know they found it and are returning it to us. Take it from me, if you want economy prices with awesome service then the Ocean Resort is a sure bet. You won't be sorry.

In my opinion, for the price it's a good place to stay.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Best in its class Let me say at the outset that I can afford much more expensive hotels, and I have stayed in them at times when the mood has suited me. However, most of the time, I just want a clean, quiet place to sleep, and I want a fair price. The Ocean Resort Waikiki suited me almost perfectly. It was close to Waikiki Beach (at the Kapiolani Park end, where I wanted to be). It allowed me to drive out of Waikiki relatively easily without fighting the traffic congestion found at the McCully or Ala Moana exit sites. My room in the Pali Tower was exactly what I had expected for the price ($74.00 per night, which included a rental car). It was a little time-worn, but nevertheless clean and comfortable, and the maid service was friendly and helpful. I really had only two complaints to speak of. First, there was no ventilation fan in the shower/toilet room. Second, the parking facilities were woefully inadequate: terribly cramped with an insufficient number of spaces. I eventually paid $7.00 per day to park at the Waikiki Banyan, kitty-corner from the Ocean Resort with its main entrance on Kuhio. As it turned out, I didn't mind the short walk, and I always found a space for my car there. Bottom line: I largely recommend the Ocean Resort in spite of the two caveats that I just mentioned, especially if, like me, you hate to spend money on frills that you'll never use. This hotel is a great choice for the economy-minded traveler.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Great, clean place to stay! Stayed at the Ocean Resort for 9 nights (July 23 - August 1). Had a kitchenette in the Pali Tower on the 5th floor. The room was very clean and the housekeeping staff were great! (A little tip everyday goes a long way!) Always cleaned our room everyday before noon. The front desk staff were always busy and when you asked them a question about buses, trolleys, or general direction information, they kinda acted like you were a bother and didn't tell you right anyway, so I quit asking. The bellmen were great. If your flight is at night (our check-out was at noon), they will keep your baggage for you. (Remember to tip!) Yes, they do tie a rope around your luggage and leave it in the lobby. BUT they are always right there watching it - it didn't bother me in the least. The swimming pools (two of them) are on the 3rd floor. They were very clean and had a nice sitting area. (The water was a little cold, however.) The resturant was good and prices were very reasonable. We ate there 3 times. I don't like crowded resturants that well - and this one was never crowded. They have internet access in the lobby. It is 15 cents per minute and you can feed cash into it. That is a little pricey but I just wanted to check my email and I always had enough time when I put $2.00 into it. There is an ABC store right next door and the beach is just a block away. You can't beat the location! It's wonderful. This hotel is not the HILTON and if you are going to Waikiki on your honeymoon, anniversary, etc., I would recommend another fancier place to stay. BUT if you just want a nice, very clean room and cheaper prices, with a WONDERFUL location, I would definetly recommend this hotel. When I go to Waikiki again, I will be staying at Ocean Resort.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Better than I expected I was extremely nervous about staying at the Ocean Resort Hotel, after reading all the reviews over the last few months. We stayed from July 13 - 22 inclusive, as I had to photograph a wedding at the Hilton Hawaiian Village on the 15th July.I was very nicely surprised with the hotel. Ok, it looks a little shabby, but, to be quite honest, so did most of Waikiki. We upgraded about 2 weeks before we left to a Kitchenette, and asked to be located as far up as possible. We were given a room on the 15th floor, that faced a hotel on the other side of the road, but I didn't really care - we were basically only in the room to sleep. We also had a car included in our room rate, which was $107 plus taxes per day.The room was huge and clean, the king sized bed was comfortable and everything in the room worked well. The shower pressure was great, the housekeeping service was done everyday and we received a complimentary Honolulu Star (I think) every morning, except Sunday. The reception staff were very helpful - and I always find that if you smile and are nice about your request, you usually always get what you want. I used the email facility in the foyer every day to contact my children and the service was efficient, and quite reasonably priced ($1 for about 7 minutes). We didn't ever eat at the restaurant, and the guy in the weird little shop downstairs eventually even said hello when I walked in (I consciously worked on charming him inot it!).I'd just like to say something about all the complaints I have read about the lifts. We stayed in the Pali Tower and when we were there, there were a lot of sporting groups with at least 50 people in each group and tour groups staying in the hotel. The longest we had to wait (and we were on the 15th floor) was about 2 minutes. Having said that, we spent a lot of time for the first 4 days we were in Waikiki at the Hilton Hawaiian preparing for the wedding I had to photograph. The lines to check into that particular resort were AT LEAST 30 people deep, every single time we were there. The Rainbow Tower, which is the tower that faces the beach and is gorgeous, has 6 lifts in them. My friends were staying on the 4th floor, and had to wait 15 minutes - that's right 15 minutes - to get a lift 4 floors down. Their room's rack rate was $550 a night....ours was $107......If you ever read about slow lifts, go and sit in the Hilton foyer for half an hour. So all in all, it was a greaty stay - we come from the Gold Coast in Queensland in Australia, which is just like Waikiki, so I'm pretty fussy about my hotels. This isn't the nicest hotel I've ever stayed in, but for the price it was excellent. This was my first trip out of Australia, and I really, truly expected a flea-ridden dog box, and was pleasantly surprised. Stay in a kitchenette room - its bigger and better equipped.Aloha!....and sorry for rambling on, but I just HAD to have my say.

<Author>sylvia1900
<Content>Better than I expected.... I stayed here for two five day stints between june 1 to 6 and the other between june 10 to 15. I came to honolulu with 3 other people so we had two rooms both times. We were fairly apprehensive as to what this hotel would be like but all our worrying was for nothing. Our first time around was fantastic. They put us in two rooms beside each other right on the top floor (14th) of the diamond tower. We didn't even have to ask!! The rooms were completely basic.....bed, tv, air conditioner, table, 2 chairs, fridge, shower, toilet, and sink but nicer than i expected....and super clean as well. Don't expect new furniture or decor because you won't get it here. Yes, things in this hotel are old and faded but that doesn't mean they are dirty. It just means they're old. Our view was great for the price we paid (80 canadian dollars a night).....probably 55 or 60 american, i'm guessing. For this price you won't get any closer to the beach which is 2 blocks away. We never went in the pool but we did check it out and its just like everybody says.....not all that appealing....but seriously who comes to hawaii to swim in a pool??? The restaurant is cheap (particularily the breakfast) but the service is nothing to rave about. We found this to be true of almost all the restaurants in hawaii though. The servers are spoiled here.....almost all the bills come with a reminder that it is american custom to leave 15 to 20 percent as a gratuity. I'm a server and am pretty lenient when it comes to judging others service but never have i so consistently had bad service ever. The best service we got was at TGI Fridays and we ate at a lot of expensive restaurants. Don't go to Cheeseburger in Paradise....worst ever!!! Ok sorry back to the hotel. To respond about others complaints.....our elevator was never slow and our hallway was extremely clean. The housekeeper always had our rooms done up by 12 or 1. But we left her 10 dollars. A little tipping goes a long way with the housekeeper. The one thing that does suck is that the showerheads are very low. If you are taller that 5 foot 5 you will have to duck your head or bend your whole body to wash your hair. When were done our first 5 nights we requested that we have the same rooms when we came back not really thinking they would make a note of it. We were pleasantly surprised to have the exact same rooms except one floor down for our second stay. Again the rooms were basic but clean. My room did have one small problem. Our drain had a minor clog in it. That is probably the worst thing I could say about my whole stay at this hotel. There are a couple other things but they are minor....you have to pay for local calls but i always used the pay phones downstairs....they were cheaper. And you have to pay for using the safe. These extra charges didn't bother me but thought i'd include it as an FYI. The hotel also has internet access at 15 cents a minute at a couple kiosks. Another hint to those on a budget.....buy yourself a hawaii area entertainment book. It will save you a ton of money if you are planning on doing all the touristy stuff and if you plan on eating out a lot. Overall I was completely satisfied with my stay here and would not hesitate to stay here again.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>A great deal I got an incredible rate on this hotel: $54/night on expedia. (Rack rates are posted as $130). It's basic but just fine. It's a high-rise--my 14th-floor room had a little balcony and a view of the back of Diamond Head. It is only 1 long block to the beach, and right on Kuhio Avenue where all the buses go--very convenient. Lots of shopping and restaurants, and tour buses stop at the adjacent Aston Waikiki. The room was small, with 2 twin beds, but very clean and comfortable, with a refrigerator. There is a small Astro-Turf pool deck with two small pools and soda machines. The hotel also has a restaurant and a gift shop, where you can rent hair dryers for $2/day (!). I'd stay there again for such a low rate.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Great value We visited honolulu and Waikiki the first week of June to celebrate our honeymoon. We stayed at the Ocean Resort and had an absolutely wonderful stay. The hotel was just like the pictures online and its of couse not the Hilton, but it was so close to the beach and for the price you couldn't beat it. We had a room on the top floor with an excellent ocean view. The carpets were fairly new and the room was spotless. The beds are like any other hotel beds, but it provided a good nights sleep. The floor in the bathroom was a little outdated, but then again, we didn't go to Hawaii to stay in the bathroom. We never ate at the restaurant, it seemed a little dead, but I can't judge the food. The staff was friendly and the rooms were always cleaned promptly. The pool area was very clean. We did laundry once and the laundromat was decent. Take your own detergent, though. It's $1.25 to wash and to dry. Plus the cost of detergent.There is an ABC Store right around the corner (and on every corner) for drinks and other items. I would highly suggest taking your own bandaids, because you'll get blisters from walking everywhere (even in your most comfy shoes). They're very expensive to buy in Waikiki. Our overall experience in this hotel was great. You can't get any closer to the beach for this price.

<Author>cleo2020
<Content>Moderate Hotel one block from Beach Desk Staff efficient, not overly helpful or friendly. Restaurant staff efficient and one was friendly. Breakfasts start at $4.15 and pancakes are surprisingly good. Safe key costs $3.50 a day. Two pools on third floor are utilitarian at best. Small additions to the pool area would make a BIG difference. Maid staff was friendly and accommodating (tipping helped). Ocean view from room looked like the one on website. Carpets were clean, elevators quick, and small fridge in room, but NO coffee maker. Hotel's west entrance is right on Bus line-north to Downtown or south to Diamond Head. Almost all tour buses pick up in front, at the Aston on Waikiki Beach or across the street at the Marriott. A convenience store is half a block away for phone cards, munchies, drinks. There are fireworks on the beach every Friday and Saturday night and a free movie on Sunday. The International Market Place is six blocks away and souvenir heaven. Best time to buy is at night between 9-11, just before it closes and vendors in the very back will give better prices. Aloha Island Tours offers good prices and will upgrade for free if they over book.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Nothing to write home about but not the worst I've stayed at This hotel was what I expected for the price. Nice location, older hotel but clean, horrible parking...but that's anywhere in Hawaii. Everyone was exactly right about the elevators being slow. A tip: If you want your room cleaned before 4pm, place the hanging placard on your door knob. One side says do not disturb the other says Please clean this room as early as possible. When we used the placard our room was clean by 12N...without it..good luck! The hotel staff was not the greatest. We arrived at 11pm Hawaii time...2am our time and the front desk staff required the signatures of every single person staying in our room....even the minors. When the signatures didn't meet his standards, they were required to sign their names again. He could not give me any explanation as to why this needed to be done. Needless to say, I had a bad taste in my mouth before we ever got checked in. The pool was nice (although extremely cold) and there was never a crowd so it was great for sunning. Since returning home, there have been additional charges placed on my credit card and no one seems to be able to explain why...still waiting on a response from the hotel. I don't think I would stay at this hotel again, as I would spend a few dollars more and stay at a nicer hotel with friendlier staff.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Excellent for the price My family and I stayed here for 6 nights in May 2004. 1.5 blocks from the beach, bus stop across the street, bus tours pick up on this street, lots of parking at the Banyan (kitty corner from hotel). We had 2 rooms. Room1 was a superior kitchenette on 9th floor of Pali tower-got for $55 per night. This room had 2 double beds, a small dining table with chairs, lots of drawer space for clothes, TV. Room2 was on 6th floor of Diamond Head tower-paid $55, but this was actually a deluxe room. This one did not have a dining table, but actually had an extra twin bed in the corner in addition to a king bed. We didn't really cook, but used the fridge and kitchen counter space. Both rooms were clean, airy, and very big. Room 1 had partial ocean view, between 2 buildings. Room 2 had a view of diamond head volcanoe. Both had lanais/balconys with plastic white chairs. I did not find the elevator that slow at all, but i guess this is an opinion which is all relative. Hotel generally has 3 people at the front desk, 1 person at the tour desk. I'm very particular about sound, and both these rooms were very quiet, even though the 400+ room hotel was completely full. I would definitely stay here again if I could get a rate of $55-$90 a night. I hope this helps!

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Well worth the money I was at the Ocean Resort in mid March on work and for some vacation. Stayed 9 nights. I travel quite a bit so I know what to expect for what you pay. I've stayed a pricey hotels and received nothing, and stayed at cheap hotels and received the kitchen sink. This hotel falls towards the middle. The price is well worth it. I stayed for only $80/night, and recieved 1 night free. The location couldn't be much better. Just a few minutes from the beach at 1 end of Waikiki. Also, it was convenient in my travels to other parts of the island for work. The room was nothing to write home about but the beds were clean, comfortable and made by time I came home each afternoon. If you are on a honeymoon, spend a few extra bucks and get a classier place, if you are jsut looking for a vacation hotel, this is easily a good choice. Who needs to stay in there room in HI other than to sleep anyways?

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Not what I expected.... I guess I will start off by saying that I have definately seen worse. BUT....This hotel was not what I had expected it to be, especially after seeing pictures and the like online on several different sites.We paid approximately $106 per night for 6 nights and got a night free (the promotion that the website that I booked on was running). Yes, most hotels on the island were pricier, but I'd rather have paid more than to stay in this hotel. To me, this was not a great value. The lobby area is quite deceiving as is the outside of the hotel. It looks pretty decent based on both areas. When we were showed our Superior Kitchenette, I was pretty suprised. Not only did it smell like mildew, as did the halls), but the kitchenette was pretty dirty. The floor was nasty and the vents were disgusting. They looked as if they hadn't been cleaned in months. There was a coffee maker and electric burners, both of which I would not use, even if someone paid me. The bathroom was also not that clean. I made a pretty disgusting discovery on the toilet seat, it was a body hair (and it wasn't from someone's head, I will say that much). The overall decore of the room (and the hotel, for that matter) was 70's. This hotel is in need of some serious renovations. Even the highchair that I had to put my son in in the hotel's restarant was the oldest model I have ever seen. We had called the front desk to complain about the condition of the room (after finding the hair). We were told that we had two choices. We could either tell housekeeping exactly what we wanted cleaned or we could downgrade to another room that was going to be on the 2nd or 3rd floor (we were currently on the 10th). So, much to our dismay, we agreed to have housekeeping come in and clean. It definately still was not as clean as it should have been.At one point during the week, we were trying to kill a flying roach that somehow got into the room. Definately not the highlight of the week.The pool area was also pathetic. There are two pools. One appeared to be quite dirty, as the water was really cloudy. The next day, it was still cloudy. Needless to say, we did not spend much time at the pool.I was highly, highly disappointed with this hotel. I was not expecting high class w/all of the amenities, but this was well below standards and hardly what I would have paid $106 per night for.We had some family staying at one of the Ohana hotels for less money. The Ohana Village hotel blew the Ocean Resort away by far in every area. It was updated, clean and refreshing.The one good thing about the Ocean Resort was the location. It was only a block from the beach and there were numerous shops and restaurants around. I will also say that the front desk staff were very nice.Well, that about sums it up. Honestly, you might be thinking that I am just a picky, picky person. I really am not. All I ask for is a clean hotel room. I am sorry, but this hotel just does not cut it. Do yourself a favor, keep researching hotels.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Ocean Resort Hotel--great value We booked this hotel as part of a package using WWTE (--------)Upon arriving we were upgraded to a room with a kingsize bed and a kitchenette. The room was a corner room with a wrap around balcony that had a partial view of the ocean. Our room was clean and roomy enough to be comfortable. The staff was very friendly and the maid service was good and we did not have a problem with our rooms being cleaned late in to the day. The elevators were not slow as some had reported but they could use a fresh coat of paint. We rented a car and parked in the Banyon garage across the street. The parking rate for the week was $30 and was going up April 16th to $40. The daily rate is going up to $7. We did not eat any meals at the hotel but the restaurant did seem to be busier than others had previously reported. I would stay here again because you are in walking distance of most things. Buses and trolleys are available to travel but if time is important then rent a car if you want to go outside of Waikiki Beach. If you want your money's worth and don't mind an older hotel then stay here, you can always visit the newer hotels and enjoy their lobbies, etc. The hotel is only a short walk to the beach and within easy walking distance of many restaurants/shops and the International Marketplace.

<Author>MaiTai
<Content>Good Value We booked through Expedia air/hotel package stayed at Ocean Resort Hotel for 5 nights (3/28-4/1). This hotel is right behind Aston Waikiki Hotel and across from Marriott. We requested connecting and non-smoking rooms but did NOT get any of these request. The lady at the front desk told us non-smoking rooms were not available at the time. They put us in the smoking units on the 4th floor, which is really noisy because of the traffic. Both of our rooms are rated as Superior Kitchenette. We were expecting a full kitchen but this was not the case. It has a mini-fridge, mini-microware, a portable electric two-burner, and a coffee maker(with no coffee). The location is excellent, 1 block from the beach and at the quiet side of Waikiki. Parking across the street at the Banyan Hotel is $5 for 24 hours. This is an older hotel but they keep it clean. Room cleaning is done at around 3PM. If you like swimming in the pool, don't stay at this hotel. The pool is on the 3nd floor and nothing is special about it. If you're going to stay her, request for 8th floor or higher. Like earlier reviews, they nickel and dime on everything. Local phone call is .75 cent. Calling card/800 number is $1 each. Internet access at the lobby is .15 cent per minute.Will we be staying here again? properly not. We like the location but the hotel is only so so. We may try Aston Waikiki or Bayan Hotel next time, which is right next to this hotel. They looked newer from the outside.

Basically, if you want a clean and friendly hotel in a great location for a budget i would suggest this place =)

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>great base for the price... We have just returned from staying in the Ocean Resort for 8 days Feb 21...29th 2004 It has a great location about 150yds from the sea front with all the eating places within 500 yds (Hamburgers in paradise 400yds away)  In the other direction literally about 50 yds away the bus (the name for hawaii`s transportation system) stops and there are many buses to and from the Honolulu area and beyond. The fare is a flat $2 anywhere on the island..2 blocks or the North Beach! beware going too far the seats have a very thin layer to comfort your rear end!  All the tour buses and free trams (to the shops)stop in the road the hotel is in which is great..most within 50 yds of the Ocean Resort. We stayed in the Pali Tower in a kitchenette room. It appears the management have been reading this site! The carpets in the lifts, at reception and in our room is practically new! There is only 2 lifts so at peak times you can wait for 2+min for it to come. I have only 3 minor complaints, 1 our electric burners only had one working and having complained to reception it never was actually replaced. 2 The maid was cleaning the room up late in the day (I mean about 4pm) most days so when you come back from a great day on the beach to shower off you had to either wait as she was doing you room or was about to so you could not really relax knowing she would come in soon! 3 As we were married it was not a problem for us but beware that the bathroom only has in it (behind a door) the toilet and bath/shower. The sink for washing/shaving and the like is in the room next to the bathroom door in full view! The garage parking at the ocean resort is a rip off $8 per night! best tip drop off your partner to make the coffee get dinner for you and go and park the car behind the Honolulu Zoo about 10 min walk away for free! Would I stay there again Yes! great for the price but not the Hilton! (or their prices!) Another tip.. the safe in your room is for hire $3 or thereabouts a day. (I think it should be free)  Do youself a favour hire it on the second day (save$3) as your flight probably will not arrive early and you will be in the room all the time so why put your valuables in a safe if you are in the room with them! on the second to last day take the key back before midnight (save anther $3) as the hire is daily. One final thought if you use the phone in your room to dial a 1-800 number they charge you $1 per call!! go downstairs pass by reception to the left there are 5 pay phones there for free. Say Hi to Carlos the Trip Advisor he knows his stuff and actually gives great advice! He told us the round island trip by the bus was great value for $2 but it will hurt your butt..he was right....and it took 4 hours painful or what.  
<Date>Mar 4, 2004

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Good for the Budget-Minded Traveler My boyfriend and I stayed at the Ocean Resort Hotel for 9 days, 2/3-2/11. It would not have been my first choice, but we were on a budget. When we arrived, we were told that there would be no air conditioning for at least two days. They gave us two bottles of water and a box of chocolate covered macadamia nuts for the inconvenience. I feared everything was going to go downhill from there. As it turned out, the air conditioning came back on as promised, and we never used it anyway. Like others before me have stated, the hotel is a bit run down and could use a face lift. However, our room was mostly clean, except for a few stains on the carpet. Location to the beach and shopping was great and the staff very helpful. The elevators were EXTREMELY slow! (If you missed the 2:15, you had to wait for the 2:35!) There are washers/dryers on the third floor, along with soda and snack machines. The pools left much to be desired, so if you are a pool person, don't stay here. We were able to extend our noon checkout time to 6:00 p.m. for an additional half-day room charge. I recommend this hotel to anyone who is looking for no-frills accommodations. It's a good deal for the money, but I will go to a Marriott or Hilton the next time I visit. Aloha!!!  
<Date>Feb 18, 2004

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Great price for a suprisingly good hotel! My wife and I stayed at this hotel for the first 3 days of our Hawaii stay. We wanted a cheaper hotel for this leg of our stay since we planned to be touring most of the time.I made reservations and requested an ocean view. They not only got us an ocean view, but we also got a car rental package through the hotel for just $10 more (good if you prefer to do some exploration yourself).The ocean view that we had was from the 12th floor and looked out between two other hotels that were closer to the beach. However, we still ended up with a great ocean view and were lucky enough to catch one of the best sunsets directly from our room.The room itself was clean, although not the newest in construction. A balcony came with the room which was nice when we sat out and had breakfast.Having a rental car was not as useful since most tours either picked you up from the hotel or was within easy walking distance. This was added to the fact that you needed to pay for parking at a nearby hotel (about $5).All in all, for the price that we paid, this was the most economical, but suprisingly pleasant hotels that we stayed in. I would stay in this hotel again for future trips to Oahu.  
<Date>Feb 3, 2004

<Content>Very pleasant hotel Stayed at the Ocean Resort Hotel my first trip to Hawaii in October 2001 and thought it was very nice. Loved the open air lobby and the orchids growing out of the rocks. The room was nothing special but nice. The staff weren't overly friendly, but pleasant enough. When we reported that our patio door didn't lock it was fixed almost imediately. If I'd make one change it would be to put new carpet in the hallways. It was very faded and stained.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Why pay more? It's not the Four Seasons, or any other hotel some of us big city types are used to... but if you pay more to stay anywhere else you're an idiot.When you're spending your days at the beach (2 blocks away), and your evenings eating, shopping, and drinking mai tais; that leaves very little time in the room. Even if you include time sitting on the oceanview lanai as we did.Sure the decor is a little dated, but they obviously try harder to keep the place clean. Housekeeping kept our room clean and full of towels. (Try tipping people! A few bucks a day goes a long way.) --Let's put it this way, I'm a germ-a-phobe, but at no point was I grossed out by this place.... I've seen worse things in a few 5 star hotels.The hotel seemed safe, our car wasn't broken into, and using the room safe adds some peace of mind.And the fridge is nice for grabbing some beverages at the ABC store down the street and sitting on the lanai.Realize early on that this is Hawaii.... everything and everyone is laid back..... including the elevators.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Location, location, location! We just got back from Hawaii and stayed at the Ocean Resort Hotel. I found it a clean, great hotel for the money. The location is GREAT! 2 blocks from the beach; one block from the zoo and a short walk to all the shopping and restaurants one could want. Also close to the International Market - a nice place to browse and buy gifts to take home. The restaurant has great prices and good food - but is a bit slow in service, so give yourself lots of time if you eat before a scheduled tour. The $3.50 a day for the safe key was well worth it. We stayed there before and after our cruise. Both rooms had a small refridgerator and ice trays (the only ice machine is on the third floor). The rooms were clean, quiet and we had no complaints. The nicest person at the desk was Kim, everybody was a bit too busy to answer questions or offer help. Ocean Resort would not allow us to pay extra for late check-out or early check-in because we booked through a travel agency. I booked the hotel through Expedia/Hotels. The bellman will keep your luggage locked next to his desk for you. We found the bellman to be quite helpful for getting us transportation when we needed and offering advice on other items. All-in-all, for the money, we couldn't have asked for much more!

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Great Place! Me again, who relied on internet pics, traveladvisor.com  price when booking a place to stay! I found the Ocean Resort Hotel a great bargain! Stayed 3 - 8 November  weather was great! Neat, clean, friendly hotel. People I met in Waikiki complained of the noise from their hotels on the main streets, but this one was nice  quiet! I left my balcony door open each night  didn't hear a thing! My room was the cheapest single room available  it was basic, but still VERY nice and who stays in anyway?! It was clean and big enough! No fabulous view, but I wasn't there for the view from my room! :) Nice queen size bed, cable t.v., table  two chairs inside room  two chairs on balcony. Aircon.  fridge. No hair dryer or coffee, but they still supplied me with shampoo/soap  clean linen everyday! I just stocked up on coffee/sugar/milk  water at the nearby ABC store. Charge of $3.50 per day for safe use in room. Two large, clean swimming pools on 3rd floor, with lounge chairs  a good view, if it's too windy to sun on the nearby beach. Staff very friendly  helpful, especially Jay, the tour organiser in the lobby! Internet access, 4 terminals,  6 phone booths also in lobby (recommend pre-paid calling card to save on costs!) Hotel is two small blocks from main drag and close to everything, including International Market, Zoo, Aquarium, Diamond Head, Trolley buses. Lots of cheap restaurants nearby for budget travellers. For info. of Aussies looking for somewhere to stay, I found that a certain well known airline travel book had this place listed for triple the price that was on Hotels.com!! My advice, shop around and use tripadvisor.com to your advantage! We don't go this far to sit in our rooms..do we?! I'll be staying here again!

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>what I expected not fancy but clean place to sleep Visited Oct 28 thru Nov 4th 2003 First time in Waikiki. Ocean resort was our choice because of price. Older Hotel but mostly clean. Rooms are very large and roomy. We stayed in the Pali Tower which has either a city view or Diamond head. Go for Diamond head less noise from the street. We were booked in the 4th floor and asked to be moved up in hopes of a view. For 10 dollars more a night we got the 18th floor. slight view of Ocean and great view of Diamond head. Great room but the elevators are SLOW would we come back ? yes if we were on a buget. But like someone said who stays in their hotel room wih the beach just a walk away......Aloha

<Author>SugarWahine
<Content>Great Location, great deal as a frequent traveler to HNL, I stayed here for a weekend away from it all. It is not glamorous and is in need of a makeover, but for the price, it is the best deal in Waikiki. Forget the pool, but who uses a pool in Waikiki? One block from the beach, very convenient an ABC store is nearby for all your water/snack needs. The room was fine, old, but clean and the staff is very accomodating, definite spirit of aloha. If you want something special or are a first time visitor, this is probably not the place, but if you are looking for bargain prices, a clean room and shower to enjoy the sights of waikiki, go for it.

<Author>ashleybrookdee
<Content>Clean, friendly, good location My husband and I just returned from here from our honeymoon. By no means is this a resort but it is nice, clean and friendly. We decieded a head of time that we did not want to spend a fortune on a hotel room we would not be spending much time in. True enough the halls and carpet are a bit worn but this is an older area and hotel. Our room was clean and in a great location only one block from the main strip and beach. The do charge $8.00 per day for parking but that is at most hotels as well. The elevators are extremly slow! But everything in Waikiki is laid back and slow including all service in resturants. Overall we had a great experiance. We recieved a free upgrade on our room as well. At $59.00 per night for an ocean view in Waikiki beach it was not bad at all.

<Author>redsilk
<Content>Bargain we stayed here in july 2003. I agree with most reviewers that the hallways needed a new coat of paint and definately new carpets!. First impressions were not that good and we had a lot of reservations about our room after. Overall the room was bigger than anticipated. There was a small kitchenette which came in quite handy to store drinks and water cold. The room was clean, carpet was new ( i think). Well at least it felt and looked new. and bathroom was clean too.The furniture style was old but clean and good condition. Some staff was friendly and more helpful than others. Don't bother with the pool which is very small. The ocean is just a 5 minute walk away. It's a little distance of a walk to the shopping areas (15minutes) but it's a pleasant walk by the beach. it's also near an abc store (convenient store) but so are all the hotels in honolulu. i would stay here again.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Ocean Resort Waikiki Just returned from a 7day vacation to Waikiki. Bought the package from Expedia together with the airport-hotel-airport transfer. Was very glad that I paid the extra $ for the transfer because Expedia staff were waiting at the gate soon as we alighted from the plane. Made everything easy and smooth. I had bought the basic no-frills package so no leis for us, which was just fine. The very friendly greeters helped us get our luggage then escorted us to the waiting shuttle, then off to the Ocean Resort. This hotel is on the eastern side of Waikiki beach, just a short walk about 1block to the beach. Its on the other side of the the Waikiki Marriott where most tour pickups are. The hotel is a bit old, carpets in the elevator really yuckky because a lot of beach sand ends up there. Housekeeping needs some improvement - my daughter had dropped a skittle candy on the floor and was still there 3 days later. But overall not a bad hotel for the price and location.All the attractions were very expensive but hey, you go all the way to Hawaii you have to spend the $. We attended the Polynesian Cultural Centre luau which cost US$89. The SS Arizona Memorial was free, but we paid for the transportation ($15.00 per person). Climbing Diamond Head was $1.00 but paid $8.00 transportation. For Hanauma Bay we decided to hop on the public bus, adults $1.75 and kids .75. We used the public buses a lot and even that got a bit expensive.The best part of Waikiki beach was the evening stroll. Most people came out after dark when it was cooler and the breeze was very relaxing. Most places stayed open past midnight, very vibrant city.I would definitely think about Hawaii again, maybe Maui for a bit of different flavour, and will definitely book through Expedia again.  
<Date>Jul 24, 2003
